         How to get the SHA-1 fingerprint certificate in Android Studio for debug mode?
        </a>
       </h1>
       <div class="ml12 aside-cta flex--item print:d-none sm:ml0 sm:mb12 sm:order-first sm:as-end">

           <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/27609442/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
            <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
             <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

         <div class="postcell post-layout--right">
          <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
           <p>
            I have shifted myself from
            <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Eclipse_%28software%29">
             Eclipse
            </a>
            to
            <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Android_Studio">
             Android Studio
            </a>
            . Now I am trying to work on my Map app. So I need my SHA-1 fingerprint certificate number.
           </p>
           <p>
            When I was using Eclipse it was right under
            <strong>
             Windows -&gt; Preferences -&gt; Android -&gt; Build
            </strong>
            . But in Android Studio I couldn't find out any option like this so that I could find easily the fingerprint. I am using Windows. I have read from this
            <a href="http://developer.android.com/tools/publishing/app-signing.html">
             link
            </a>
            that:
           </p>
           <blockquote>
            <p>
             Android Studio signs your app in debug mode automatically when you
  run or debug your project from the IDE.
            </p>
           </blockquote>
           <p>
            So I tried to run this in command line after setting my Java bin path from
            <a href="http://pongodev.com/get-sha1-for-debug/">
             this link
            </a>
            and unfortunately couldn't find my fingerprint.
            <strong>
             It is saying that it is an illegal option
            </strong>
            .
           </p>
           <pre><code>keytool -list -v -keystore "%USERPROFILE%\.android\debug.keystore" -alias androiddebugkey -storepass android -keypass android
</code></pre>
           <p>
            Is there a way to find the SHA-1 fingerprint from Android Studio like it was very easy in Eclipse? As I am newbie in Android Studio, what is the full process to find it?
           </p>
           <p>
            Another thing I want to add is that I have my Eclipse generates the SHA-1 fingerprint and previously I have my app registered on that fingerprint in Google developer console, and I worked on that app in Eclipse by that API key. Is the same API key can be worked on this my project in Android Studio?
           </p>
          </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="34223470">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="1456" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             1456
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>

              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             <strong>
              Easiest ways ever:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <h2>
             Update added for Android Studio V 2.2 in last step
            </h2>
            <p>
             There are two ways to do this.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              1. Faster way
             </strong>
             :
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              Open Android Studio
             </li>
             <li>
              Open your Project
             </li>
             <li>
              Click on Gradle (From Right Side Panel, you will see
              <strong>
               Gradle Bar
              </strong>
              )
             </li>
             <li>
              Click on Refresh (Click on Refresh from
              <strong>
               Gradle Bar
              </strong>
              , you will see
              <strong>
               List
              </strong>
              Gradle scripts of your Project)
             </li>
             <li>
              Click on Your Project (Your Project Name form
              <strong>
               List
              </strong>
              (root))
             </li>
             <li>
              Click on Tasks
             </li>
             <li>
              Click on Android
             </li>
             <li>
              Double Click on signingReport (You will get
              <strong>
               SHA1
              </strong>
              and
              <strong>
               MD5
              </strong>
              in
              <strong>
               Run Bar
              </strong>
              (Sometimes it will be in Gradle Console))
             </li>
             <li>
              Select
              <strong>
               app
              </strong>
              module from
              <strong>
               module selection dropdown
              </strong>
              to run or debug your application
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Check the screenshot below:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/ZG7rI.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/ZG7rI.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              2. Work with Google Maps Activity
             </strong>
             :
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              Open Android Studio
             </li>
             <li>
              Open Your Project
             </li>
             <li>
              Click on
              <strong>
               File
              </strong>
              menu -&gt; Select
              <strong>
               New
              </strong>
              -&gt; Click on
              <strong>
               Google
              </strong>
              -&gt; Select
              <strong>
               Google Maps Activity
              </strong>
             </li>
             <li>
              A dialog would appear -&gt; Click on
              <strong>
               Finish
              </strong>
             </li>
             <li>
              Android Studio would automatically generate an
              <strong>
               XML
              </strong>
              file
              <strong>
               named
              </strong>
              with
              <code>
               google_maps_api.xml
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              You would get
              <strong>
               debug SHA1
              </strong>
              key here (at
              <strong>
               line number 10
              </strong>
              of the XML file)
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Check Screenshot below:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/u4Ppn.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="Enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/u4Ppn.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <h2>
             Android Studio V 2.2 Update
            </h2>
            <p>
             There is an issue with
             <strong>
              Execution
             </strong>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Solution:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              Click on
              <strong>
               Toggle tasks execution/text mode
              </strong>
              from
              <strong>
               Run bar
              </strong>
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Check Screenshot below:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/UG1vW.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/UG1vW.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Done.
             </strong>
            </p>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="27639043">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="333" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             333
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

              </path>
             </svg>

            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/27639043/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

             </svg>
            </a>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             My problem is the same as I have also shifted my
             <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Google_Maps">
              Google Maps
             </a>
             project from
             <strong>
              Eclipse
             </strong>
             to
             <strong>
              Android Studio
             </strong>
             . I have solved my problem by following this:
            </p>
            <p>
             Go to your Java bin directory via the command:
            </p>
            <pre><code>C:\Program Files\Java\jdk1.7.0_71\bin&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Now type in the below command in your command window (CMD.EXE):
            </p>
            <pre><code>keytool -list -v -keystore c:\users\your_user_name\.android\debug.keystore -alias androiddebugkey -storepass android -keypass android
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Example:
            </p>
            <pre><code>keytool -list -v -keystore c:\users\James\.android\debug.keystore -alias androiddebugkey -storepass android -keypass android
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Or you can just write this in cmd if you don't know the username:
            </p>
            <pre><code>keytool -list -v -keystore "%USERPROFILE%\.android\debug.keystore" -alias androiddebugkey -storepass android -keypass android
</code></pre>
            <p>
             And you will get the SHA1.
            </p>
            <p>
             Then I created a new key from
             <a href="https://code.google.com/apis/console">
              https://code.google.com/apis/console
             </a>
             because of my package name got changed and then use this key in my application. It works fine.
            </p>
            <p>
             Make sure you are in
             <strong>
              BIN
             </strong>
             folder of
             <strong>
              jdkX.X.X_XX (my folder name is jdk1.7.0_71)
             </strong>
             , or else if you don't know what folder name you have then find it by opening the Java folder, and you will see what the folder name is, but you must be in your BIN folder and then run this command. Today I have got my SHA1 value in a cmd command window by the above procedure.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              SNAPSHOT:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             <img alt="Enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/RTBBF.png"/>
            </p>
           </div>

               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 I couldn't copy the SHA1 from the CMD so I moved the whole output of your given command to a file by adding:
                 <code>
                  &gt; output.txt
                 </code>
                 behind your command. You can also add
                 <code>
                  | clip
                 </code>
                 behind the command. You will get the output of the command in your Windows Clipboard. I hope it also saves time for others.
                 <a href="http://www.labnol.org/software/copy-command-output-to-clipboard/2506/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                  More info about using | clip
                 </a>
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/4815184/sjoerd-pottuit" title="2,157 reputation">
                  Sjoerd Pottuit
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2016-01-05 14:58:37Z, License: CC BY-SA 3.0">
                  Jan 5, 2016 at 14:58
                 </span>
                </span>
                <span title="this comment was edited 2 times">
                 <svg aria-hidden="true" class="va-text-bottom o50 svg-icon iconPencilSm" height="14" viewbox="0 0 14 14" width="14">
                  <path d="m11.1 1.71 1.13 1.12c.2.2.2.51 0 .71L11.1 4.7 9.21 2.86l1.17-1.15c.2-.2.51-.2.71 0ZM2 10.12l6.37-6.43 1.88 1.88L3.88 12H2v-1.88Z">
                  </path>
                 </svg>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="59948755" data-comment-owner-id="308836" data-comment-score="1" id="comment-59948755">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="cool" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">
                 1
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 @SPottuit: Interesting tip for
                 <code>
                  clip.exe
                 </code>
                 , din't know it existed, thanks. Also, removing
                 <code>
                  -v
                 </code>
                 will give you the SHA1 only as output, or on Windows you can pipe the output from -v through
                 <code>
                  | find "SHA1" | clip
                 </code>
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="67866731">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/67866731/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Many Users has given their answers and it's working fine in Android Studio's version below 4.2. But for
             <em>
              <strong>
               Android Studio 4.2
              </strong>
             </em>
             and newer version ,follows these steps to generate
             <em>
              <strong>
               SHA Key
              </strong>
             </em>
             . Steps are given in these pictures.
            </p>
            <p>
             <em>
              <strong>
               Steps:-
              </strong>
             </em>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              1)
             </strong>
             Click on the
             <strong>
              gradle
             </strong>
             . Top right on the
             <strong>
              Android Studio
             </strong>
             . As you can see in this picture.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/6EHfL.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="Step1" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/6EHfL.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              2)
             </strong>
             Now click on
             <strong>
              icon
             </strong>
             as seen in below picture. A new
             <strong>
              searchable windows/screen will open
             </strong>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/eeB3n.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="SHA2" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/eeB3n.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              3)
             </strong>
             Now type,
             <em>
              <strong>
               gradle signingreport
              </strong>
             </em>
             and press
             <strong>
              Enter
             </strong>
             to start generating
             <strong>
              SHA KEY
             </strong>
             as seen in below picture.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/1pkVW.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="sha3" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/1pkVW.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              4)
             </strong>
             <strong>
              Your
              <strong>
               SHA Key
              </strong>
              will generate as seen in this picture. Using these steps you can generate SHA KEY in Android Studio 4.2.
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/BoeGz.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="sha4" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/BoeGz.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              <em>
               Note:-
              </em>
              If you are not able to get SHA key then follow instructions given in this answer.(FLUTTER/React Native ...)
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             Link:-
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/51845559/generate-sha-1-for-flutter-react-native-android-native-app/54342861#54342861">
              SHA Key for flutter/react native
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             For Mac, this worked perfectly:
            </p>
            <pre><code>keytool -list -v -keystore ~/.android/debug.keystore -alias androiddebugkey -storepass android -keypass android
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I just found the case to get SHA-1 in Android Studio:
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              Click on your package and choose
              <em>
               New
              </em>
              -&gt;
              <em>
               Google
              </em>
              -&gt;
              <em>
               Google Maps Activity
              </em>
             </li>
             <li>
              Android Studio redirects you to google_maps_api.xml
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             And you will see all you need to get
             <code>
              google_maps_key
             </code>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             <img alt="Image" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/wpLLt.png"/>
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="36257777" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="27609442" data-position-on-page="6" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="57" id="answer-36257777" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="36257777">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="57" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             57
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/36257777/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             The best solution for generating an
             <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SHA-1" rel="noreferrer">
              SHA-1
             </a>
             key for Android is from
             <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Android_Studio" rel="noreferrer">
              Android Studio
             </a>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             Click on Gradle on the far right side:
            </p>
            <p>
             <img alt="" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/eBPji.png"/>
            </p>
            <p>
             Click on the refresh icon, and you will see the name of the app:
            </p>
            <p>
             <img alt="" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/eCVpQ.png"/>
            </p>
            <p>
             Click on
             <em>
              Tasks
             </em>
             -&gt;
             <em>
              Report
             </em>
             -&gt;
             <em>
              Signing Report
             </em>
             :
            </p>
            <p>
             <img alt="" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/2XrxZ.png"/>
            </p>
            <p>
             Find the SHA-1 key on the bottom part in the console:
            </p>
            <p>
             <img alt="" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/0U468.png"/>
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="41237244">

             47
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

              </path>
             </svg>

            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/41237244/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             <strong>
              [Updated 2017]
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Step 1: On Top Right side of Android Studio Click On Gradle option.
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/aNfIl.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="Android Studio Click On Gradle option" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/aNfIl.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Step 2:
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             -- Click on Refresh (Click on Refresh from Gradle Bar, you will see List Gradle scripts of your Project)
            </p>
            <p>
             -- Click on Your Project (Your Project Name form List (root))
            </p>
            <p>
             -- Click on Tasks
            </p>
            <p>
             -- Click on Android
            </p>
            <p>
             -- Double Click on signingReport (You will get SHA1 and MD5 in Gradle Console/Run Bar)
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/T9sug.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/T9sug.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Step 3: Click on the Gradle Console option present bottom of Android Studio to see your SHA1 Key.
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/7tUtp.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/7tUtp.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Step 4:
             </strong>
             Now you got the SHA key but you can't run your project.That is why Change your configuration to app mode. See image below.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/jqt6Q.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/jqt6Q.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Like this.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/nqigX.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/nqigX.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Step 5: Happy Coding!!
             </strong>
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="68587380" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="27609442" data-position-on-page="8" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="47" id="answer-68587380" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="68587380">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             In Android studio 4+ (not sure about version), if you click on
             <code>
              Gradle
             </code>
             on the right bar, it won't show you any option to generate signing report. It will show you this:
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/eMgQT.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/eMgQT.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Click on
             <code>
              Task list not built...
             </code>
             info and un-check the option
             <code>
              Do not build gradle task list..
             </code>
             and save the settings.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/GMlk5.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/GMlk5.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Then click gradle sync button:
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/k7ow3.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/k7ow3.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Then you'll see the signingreport option:
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/G0r5B.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/G0r5B.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="37337469">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/37337469/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I did this way:
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Step 1:
             </strong>
             Go to this folder
            </p>
            <pre><code>On Mac: /Users/&lt;username&gt;/.android/

On Windows: C:\Documents and Settings\&lt;username&gt;\.android\

On Linux: ~/.android/
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Step 2:
             </strong>
             Run this command line:
            </p>
            <pre><code>keytool -list -v -keystore debug.keystore -storepass android
</code></pre>
            <p>
             You will see the SHA-1 key.
            </p>
           </div>

             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/64479657/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             for me the shortest way is to type
             <code>
              ./gradlew signingReport
             </code>
             in the terminal command line.
            </p>
            <p>
             P.s : if you are in Windows use
             <code>
              .\gradlew signingReport
             </code>
             instead.
            </p>
           </div>

            <p>
             <strong>
              For Linux &amp; Mac
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code>keytool -list -v -keystore ~/.android/debug.keystore -alias androiddebugkey -storepass android -keypass android 
</code></pre>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you just want to view the SHA certificate values then you can just run from the android folder:
            </p>
            <p>
             Step: 1
            </p>
            <pre><code>cd android
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Step: 2
            </p>
            <pre><code> ./gradlew signingReport
</code></pre>
            <p>
             ...that'll give you a quick and easy view of your fingerprint
            </p>
           </div>

            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/46767856/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <ol>
             <li>
              Click on Gradle Icon in Right Pane.
             </li>
             <li>
              Click on Root Project Name.
             </li>
             <li>
              Click Tasks
             </li>
             <li>
              Click Android
             </li>
             <li>
              Click signingReport
             </li>
             <li>
              in bottom pane where you see Run report
             </li>
             <li>
              Click "Toggle Tasks Execytions/text mode"
             </li>
             <li>
              you can see the sha-1
             </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/wIxuX.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="Android Studio SHA-1" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/wIxuX.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

            <p>
             I directly used the following command from my Mac using the terminal. I got SHA1 Finger. This is the command:
            </p>
            <pre><code>keytool -list -v -keystore ~/.android/debug.keystore -alias androiddebugkey -storepass android -keypass android
</code></pre>

        <a name="68961992">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="68961992" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="27609442" data-position-on-page="16" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="10" id="answer-68961992" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="68961992">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="10" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             10
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/68961992/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Recently Android Studio and in its last update
             <strong>
              <code>
               2020.3.1
              </code>
             </strong>
             has removed
             <code>
              signingReport
             </code>
             from Gradle sidebar but you can still get these details in Android studio in
             <code>
              Terminal
             </code>
             , just write the following command:
             <br/>
             <br/>
             <strong>
              Windows
             </strong>
             :
             <br/>
            </p>
            <pre><code>keytool -list -v -keystore "%USERPROFILE%\.android\debug.keystore" -alias androiddebugkey -storepass android -keypass android
</code></pre>
            <br/>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Linux &amp; MacOS
             </strong>
             :
             <br/>
            </p>
            <pre><code>keytool -list -v -keystore ~/.android/debug.keystore -alias androiddebugkey -storepass android -keypass android 
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2021-08-28T06:46:09" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>
             <div class="flex--item mr16" style="flex: 1 1 100px;">

                <div class="flex--item">
                 <a class="js-share-link js-gps-track" data-controller="se-share-sheet" data-gps-track="post.click({ item: 2, priv: 0, post_type: 2 })" data-s-popover-placement="bottom-start" data-se-share-sheet-license-name="CC BY-SA 4.0" data-se-share-sheet-license-url="https%3a%2f%2fcreativecommons.org%2flicenses%2fby-sa%2f4.0%2f" data-se-share-sheet-location="2" data-se-share-sheet-post-type="answer" data-se-share-sheet-social="facebook twitter " data-se-share-sheet-subtitle="" data-se-share-sheet-title="Share a link to this answer" href="/a/68961992" itemprop="url" rel="nofollow" title="Short permalink to this answer">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="36090532" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="27609442" data-position-on-page="17" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="9" id="answer-36090532" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="36090532">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="9" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             9
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/36090532/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             It's very very easy in
             <strong>
              <em>
               Gnu/Linux
              </em>
              -
              <em>
               Mac
              </em>
              -
              <em>
               Windows
              </em>
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              First:
             </strong>
             - copy this command
            </p>
            <pre><code>keytool -list -v -keystore ~/.android/debug.keystore -alias androiddebugkey -storepass android -keypass android 
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Second:
             </strong>
             Now copy and paste the command in the terminal the Android Studio
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/u95gH.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/u95gH.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Result!
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/YvRwu.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/YvRwu.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Good Luck!!
             </strong>
            </p>
           </div>

        <a name="32620298">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="32620298" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="27609442" data-position-on-page="18" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="9" id="answer-32620298" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="32620298">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="9" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             9
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/32620298/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             For getting SHA1 for a production keystore:
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              <p>
               Build --&gt; Generate Signed APK...
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Create keystore with password and follow the steps
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Go to your Mac/Library/Java/JavaVirtualMachines/jdk1.8.0_20.jdk/Contents/Home/bin and drag the bin folder to the terminal after cd command to point at it so you can use the keytool tool. So, in terminal write
               <code>
                cd
               </code>
               (drag bin here) then press enter.
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Then, copy and paste this in the terminal:
              </p>
              <pre><code>keytool -exportcert -alias Your_keystore_AliasName -keystore /Users/Home/Development/AndroidStudioProjects/YoutubeApp/app/YoutubeApp_keystore.jks -list -v
</code></pre>
              <p>
               Erase my path and go where you stored your keystore and drag your keystone and drop it after
               <code>
                -keystore
               </code>
               in the command line so the path will get created.
              </p>
              <p>
               Also, erase Your_keystore_AliaseName to put your alias keystone name that you used when you created it.
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               Press
               <kbd>
                Enter
               </kbd>
               and enter the password :)
              </p>
             </li>
             <li>
              <p>
               When you enter the password, the terminal won't show that it receives keyboard entries, but it actually does, so put the password and press
               <kbd>
                Enter
               </kbd>
               even if you don't see the password is typed out.
              </p>
             </li>
            </ol>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="31093348" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="27609442" data-position-on-page="19" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="9" id="answer-31093348" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="31093348">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="9" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             9
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/31093348/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you are using Android Studio, you can get the
             <strong>
              SHA-1 and MD5 certificate
             </strong>
             fingerprint (debug, release...
             <strong>
              all Build Types
             </strong>
             !!) fast through
             <strong>
              Gradle Tasks
             </strong>
             :
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              signingReport
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             The SHA-1 and MD5 certificates are shown in
             <strong>
              Messages Logs
             </strong>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             Android Plugin (configured in the Gradle app) creates a debug mode for default.
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              com.android.application
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             File route to keystore:
            </p>
            <pre><code>HOME/.android/debug.keystore
</code></pre>
            <p>
             I recommend to
             <strong>
              attach
             </strong>
             <code>
              debug.keystore
             </code>
             to
             <code>
              build.gradle
             </code>
             . To do this put a file,
             <code>
              debug.keystore
             </code>
             , in an app folder and then Add SigningConfigs in
             <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gradle" rel="nofollow">
              Gradle
             </a>
             app:
            </p>
            <pre><code>apply plugin: 'com.android.application'

    android {
        ................
        signingConfigs {
            debug {
                storeFile file("../app/debug.keystore")
                storePassword "android"
                keyAlias "androiddebugkey"
                keyPassword "android"
            }
            release {
                storeFile file("../app/debug.keystore")
                storePassword "android"
                keyAlias "androiddebugkey"
                keyPassword "android"
            }
        }
        ........
    }
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Extra: If you want creates for release, put a file,
             <code>
              release.keystore
             </code>
             , in an app folder. (This example uses the same
             <code>
              debug.keystore
             </code>
             .)
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

             Above answers give me a command not found error
The correct terminal command that works for me was
            </p>
            <pre><code>./gradlew signingReport
</code></pre>

               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 You can press CTRL+Enter after this command, as recommended by Android Studio.
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/7797911/mahmoud-ayman" title="1,109 reputation">
                  Mahmoud Ayman
                 </a>
                </div>

                  Jan 31 at 11:32
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
            </ul>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="34150985">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              I found a very easy process to find you MD5, SHA-1 fingerprint using
  Android Studio.
             </p>
             <ol>
              <li>
               Run your project
              </li>
              <li>
               Go to Gradle Menu (Menu: View -&gt; Tool Windows -&gt; Gradle)
              </li>
              <li>
               Go to 'signingReport' in Gradle window. (Your project -&gt; Tasks -&gt; android -&gt; signingReport)
              </li>
              <li>
               Run it. (Using double-click or Ctrl + Shift + F10)
              </li>
              <li>
               In Run window you will find all info.
              </li>
             </ol>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             It's work only for debug mode. In realease mode I can not see sha-1.
Here result of
             <code>
              gradlew signingReport
             </code>
            </p>
            <pre><code>Variant: release
Config: none
----------
Variant: releaseUnitTest
Config: none
----------
Variant: debug
Config: debug
Store: path\Android\avd\.android\debug.keystore
Alias: AndroidDebugKey
MD5: xx:xx:xx:62:86:B7:9C:BC:FB:AD:C8:C6:64:69:xx:xx
SHA1: xx:xx:xx:xx:0F:B0:82:86:1D:14:0D:AF:67:99:58:1A:01:xx:xx:xx
Valid until: Friday, July 19, 2047
----------
</code></pre>
            <p>
             So I must use keytool to get sha-1. Here official Firebase doc:
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://developers.google.com/android/guides/client-auth" rel="noreferrer">
              Get_sha-1_for_release
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="68388263">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="8" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             8
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">

              </path>
             </svg>

             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/68388263/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             For
             <strong>
              Android Studio 4.2
             </strong>
             or new
            </p>
            <p>
             Goto the
             <strong>
              Gradle
             </strong>
             on the right side
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/817ZM.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/817ZM.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Open it and then Click on
             <strong>
              Execute Gradle Task
             </strong>
             and this pan is open
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/1rD0O.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/1rD0O.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             then you have to type
             <strong>
              signingreport
             </strong>
             and press
             <strong>
              enter
             </strong>
             this will execute the command and will provide the result.
            </p>
            <p>
             For
             <strong>
              Older Version of Android Studio
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             You can follow all of the above steps on the older version to get your result.
            </p>
           </div>

             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/35715340/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             This worked in my case: Use
             <strong>
              %USERPROFILE%
             </strong>
             instead of giving path .keystore file stored in this path automatically
             <strong>
              C:Users/user name/.android
             </strong>
             :
            </p>
            <pre><code>keytool -list -v -keystore "%USERPROFILE%\.android\debug.keystore" -alias androiddebugkey -storepass android -keypass android
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you have
             <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Android_Studio" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              Android Studio
             </a>
             then it is very very simple. Just create a MapActivity using Android Studio and after creating it go into google_maps_api.xml. In there there will be a link given in comments. If you paste it in your browser, it will ask a few details to be filled in and after that your API will be generated. There is no need of using keytool and all.
            </p>
            <p>
             Screen shot:
            </p>
            <p>
             <img alt="Enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/Jrp0g.png"/>
            </p>
           </div>

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/69826701/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Click on the Terminal icon on the bottom left corner
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/3oU4h.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="Terminal" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/3oU4h.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             cd to the android folder and run
            </p>
            <pre><code>gradlew signingreport

</code></pre>
            <p>
             Once this is done, it will print the SHA-1, MD5, and SHA-256 keys
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

            <p>
             Click the Gradle icon on the right panel, then click on the (root).
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              Tasks &gt; android &gt; signingReport
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             Then the Gradle script will execute, and you will see your keys.
            </p>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="33163328" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="27609442" data-position-on-page="27" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="5" id="answer-33163328" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="33163328">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="5" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             5
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/33163328/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             For
             <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Windows_10" rel="nofollow">
              Windows 10
             </a>
             , from the
             <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Android_Studio" rel="nofollow">
              Android Studio
             </a>
             terminal:
            </p>
            <pre><code>keytool -exportcert -alias androiddebugkey -keystore %USER_PROFILE%"/.android/debug.keystore -list -v
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Note: For the
             <code>
              debug.keystore
             </code>
             , the password is "android". The debug keystore is typically located at
             <code>
              "%USER_PROFILE%"/.android/debug.keystore
             </code>
             .
            </p>
           </div>

             Use simple command:
            </p>
            <p>
             keytool -exportcert -keystore path-to-debug-or-production-keystore -list -v
            </p>
            <p>
             and you will get the SHA1 key.

            <p>
             I want to add one thing with the answer given by
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/users/3486462/softcoder">
              Softcoder
             </a>
             . I have seen some people couldn't give their
             <strong>
              debug.keystore
             </strong>
             path correctly on the
             <code>
              command line
             </code>
             . They see that they are doing the exact process accepted above, but it is not working. At that point try to drag the debug.keystore and drop it on the command line. It will help if the accepted answer is not working for you. Do the full process without any hesitation. It was a nice answer.
            </p>
